<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tridēns</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">trēs</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">three</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">dēns</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tooth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***trill.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:trill.html>trill</a> (52996)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:trillen.html>trillen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:trillo.html>trillo</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">trillare</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no"><a href = vnd.unilang:trillen.html>trille</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">trilla</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:trill.html>trill</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:trills.html>trills</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A rapid alternation between an indicated note and the one above it, in musical notation usually indicated with the <a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>letters</a> <i>tr</i> written above the staff.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">phonetics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A type of consonantal sound that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> produced by vibrations of the tongue against the place of articulation: for example, Spanish <i>rr</i>.</li>
<li>A tremulous high-pitched vocal sound produced by <a href = vnd.unilang:cats.html>cats</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:trill.html>trill</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:trills.html>trills</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:trilling.html>trilling</a></b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">trilled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To create a <a href = vnd.unilang:trill.html>trill</a> sound; to utter <a href = vnd.unilang:trills.html>trills</a> or a <a href = vnd.unilang:trill.html>trill</a>; to play or sing in tremulous vibrations of sound; to have a trembling sound; to quaver.
<ul><li><b>1692</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Dryden" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:John Dryden">John Dryden</a>, <i>Cleomenes, the Spartan Hero, a Tragedy</i>
<dl><dd>To judge of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:trilling.html>trilling</a></b> notes and tripping <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To impart the quality of a <a href = vnd.unilang:trill.html>trill</a> to; to utter as, or with, a <a href = vnd.unilang:trill.html>trill</a>.
<dl><dd><i>to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:trill.html>trill</a></b> a note, or the letter <a href = vnd.unilang:r.html>r</a></i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1730</b>, James Thomson, <i>Seasons <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a> Summer</i>
<dl><dd>The sober-suited songstress <b><a href = vnd.unilang:trills.html>trills</a></b> her lay.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To trickle.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1603</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michel_de_Montaigne" class="extiw" title="w:Michel de Montaigne"><a href = vnd.unilang:michel.html>Michel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:montaigne.html>Montaigne</a></a>,  chapter 30, in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/John_Florio" class="extiw" title="w:John Florio">John Florio</a>, transl., <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Essays_(Montaigne)" class="extiw" title="w:Essays (Montaigne)">The Essayes,<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">[</span></span><span title="or, Morall, Politike and Millitarie Discourses of Lo. Michaell de Montaigne, Knight of the Noble Order of St. Michaell, and One of the Gentlemen in Ordinary of the French King, Henry the Third His Chamber">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b"><span style="font-style: normal;">]</span></span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span></a></cite>, book II, printed at London |  By <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Valentine_Simmes" class="extiw" title="w:Valentine Simmes"><a href = vnd.unilang:val.html>Val</a>[entine] Simmes</a> for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Edward Blount</a><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span><span title="dwelling in Paules churchyard">…</span><span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"></span>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/946730821">946730821</a></small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">I come now from seeing of a shepheard at <i>Medoc</i><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span>who <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> no signe at all of genitorie parts: But where they should be, are three little <a href = vnd.unilang:holes.html>holes</a>, by which his water doth continually <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tril.html>tril</a></b> from him.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><i><abbr title="circa">c.</abbr></i> <b>1603–1606</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="w:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/King_Lear" class="extiw" title="w:King Lear">The <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedie.html>Tragedie</a> of King Lear</a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. William Shakespeares Comedies, <a href = vnd.unilang:histories.html>Histories</a>, amp; <a href = vnd.unilang:tragedies.html>Tragedies</a>: Published <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>According</a> to the True Originall <a href = vnd.unilang:copies.html>Copies</a></cite> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/First_Folio" class="extiw" title="w:First Folio">First Folio</a>), London |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Jaggard" class="extiw" title="w:William Jaggard">Isaac Iaggard</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Blount" class="extiw" title="w:Edward Blount">Ed[ward] Blount</a>, published 1623, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/606515358">606515358</a></small>, [Act IV, scene iii]:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">And now and then an ample tear <b>trilled</b> down / Her delicate cheek.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by <a href = vnd.unilang:glover.html>Glover</a> and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>Whispered <a href = vnd.unilang:sounds.html>sounds</a> / Of waters, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:trilling.html>trilling</a></b> from the riven stone.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To twirl.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:trillend.html>trillend</a> (35545)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:troefkaart.html>troefkaart</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:troefkaarten.html>troefkaarten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:troefkaart.html>troefkaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a trump card, trump</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> an advantage kept hidden</li></ol>

***trog.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:trog.html>trog</a> (27383)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">troch</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:trog.html>trog</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*trugą</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*trugaz</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">trôch</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">trough</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:trog.html>Trog</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">tråg</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dru-kó</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Irish">Middle Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="mga">drochta</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wooden basin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Classical_Armenian" class="extiw" title="w:Classical Armenian">Old Armenian</a></span> <i class="Armn mention" lang="xcl">տարգալ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="xcl-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">targal</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ladle, spoon</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), enlargement of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*dóru</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tree</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trog.html>trog</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:troggen.html>troggen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trog.html>trogje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">trough</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">trench</span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:trog.html>trog</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:trok.html>trok</a> (2248)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trekken.html>trekken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to pull; (air flow) to draft</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trok.html>trok</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trokken.html>trokken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trok.html>trokje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl">troksken</b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tocht.html>tocht</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trek.html>trek</a></span></span></dd>

***trol.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:trol.html>trol</a> (16324)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">troll</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">troll</i>. The sense "person who provokes" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Semantic_loan" class="extiw" title="w:Semantic loan">semantic loan</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">troll</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drol.html>drol</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mythological giant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trol.html>trol</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trollen.html>trollen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trol.html>trolletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">θρόμβωσις</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">thrómbōsis</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">curdling, clotting</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***trommelaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:trommelaar.html>trommelaar</a> (67053)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>from the root of <a href = vnd.unilang:trommelen.html>trommelen</a> 'to drum, ruffle' (from <a href = vnd.unilang:trommel.html>trommel</a> 'a drum') + -aar '<a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a>'
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trommelaar.html>trommelaar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trommelaar.html>trommelaars</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trommelaar.html>trommelaartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:drummer.html>drummer</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:percussionist.html>percussionist</a></li>
<li>Someone who <a href = vnd.unilang:drums.html>drums</a> (nervously) with his <a href = vnd.unilang:fingers.html>fingers</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An animal which <a href = vnd.unilang:drums.html>drums</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:drills.html>drills</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> a similar sound, notably woodpecker, cockroach and a pigeon specious</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***trompet.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:trompet.html>trompet</a> (12199)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:trompet.html>trompet</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">trompette</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">trumpet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">trompe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horn, trump, trumpet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*trumpa</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*trumba</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">trumpet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Akin to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">trumpa</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">trumba</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">horn, trumpet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tromme</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">drum</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">trumme</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">drum</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trompet.html>trompet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trompetten.html>trompetten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trompet.html>trompetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">trumpet</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:trompetter.html>trompetter</a> (35541)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:trompetter.html>trompetter</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trompetten.html>trompetten</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trompetter.html>trompetter</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:trompetters.html>trompetters</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A trumpet player, especially in an army or an a ceremony.
<ul><li><b>1973</b>, Lennaert Nijgh, "Jan Klaassen <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:trompetter.html>trompetter</a>", performed by Rob <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Nijs, <i>In <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uren.html>uren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:middag.html>middag</a></i>.

vnd.unilang:tot.html>tot</a> Den Briel / <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>geld</a> ***tronie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tronie.html>tronie</a> (55726)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">troenie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">trogne</i>, possibly ultimately from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Celtic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Celtic languages">Celtic</a></span> language, for which a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gaulish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gaulish language">Gaulish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cel-gau">*trugna</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> proposed (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">trwyn</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tronie.html>tronie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tronies.html>tronies</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tronie.html>tronietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">art</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A depiction of a person’s face with an expressive, often unflattering expression<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a face, especially one with an unpleasant or unprepossessing look or expression
<ul><li><b>2003</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arthur_Japin" class="extiw" title="w:Arthur Japin">Arthur Japin</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schitterend.html>schitterend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebrek.html>gebrek</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Arbeiderspers, Amsterdam – <a href = vnd.unilang:antwerpen.html>Antwerpen</a>, p. 226
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:redding.html>redding</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dacht.html>dacht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dus.html>dus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:tronie.html>tronie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:danken.html>danken</a>.
<dl><dd>This salvation, I thought, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> due to this mug of mine.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
